<div class="mf-section-0" id="mf-section-0">
<p>Writing a script is a great way to stretch your creativity by making a short film, movie, or <a href="/Write-a-Television-Show-Script" title="Write a Television Show Script">TV show</a>. Each script starts with a good premise and plot that takes your characters on a life-changing adventure. With a lot of hard work and <a href="/Write-a-Properly-Formatted-Screenplay" title="Write a Properly Formatted Screenplay">correct formatting</a>, you can write your own script in just a few months!
</p>

<div class="section steps   sticky">
<h3 class="in-block block_header">
<div class="altblock"><div>Part <span>1</span>
</div>
</div>
<span class="mw-headline" id="Creating-a-Story-World"><div class="method_label">Part 1 of 5:</div>Creating a Story World</span>
</h3>
<div id="steps_2" class="section_text">
<ol class="steps_list_2">
<li id="step-id-00">
<a name="step_1_1" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-1-Version-4.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 1" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/3/35/Write-a-Script-Step-1-Version-4.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-1-Version-4.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="7423632a01a1dbec89a32919d98b3dee" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/35/Write-a-Script-Step-1-Version-4.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-1-Version-4.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('7423632a01a1dbec89a32919d98b3dee')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 1" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/35/Write-a-Script-Step-1-Version-4.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-1-Version-4.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/3/35/Write-a-Script-Step-1-Version-4.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-1-Version-4.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="7423632a01a1dbec89a32919d98b3dee"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/3\/35\/Write-a-Script-Step-1-Version-4.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-1-Version-4.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/3\/35\/Write-a-Script-Step-1-Version-4.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-1-Version-4.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;\u00a9 2022 wikiHow, Inc. This image may not be used by other entities without the express written consent of wikiHow, Inc.&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_0" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_0" class="sv_vote">26</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">1</div><div class="step" id="ac8fecb05cd1fa3b1869303e639736cd">
<b class="whb">Think of a theme or conflict that you want to tell in your story.</b> Use a "What if?" question to form the idea of your script. Start taking inspiration from the world around you and ask yourself how it would be affected by a specific event or character. You may also think about an overall theme, such as love, family, or friendship for your story so that your whole script is tied together.<sup id="_ref-1" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 1"><a href="#_note-1">[1]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden="" id="ts_popup_1" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup>
<ul>
<li>For example, "What if you went back in time and met your parents when they were your age?" is the premise for <i>Back to the Future</i>, while "What if a monster rescued a princess instead of a handsome prince?" is the premise to <i>Shrek</i>.</li>
<li>Carry a small notebook with you wherever you go so you can take down notes when you get ideas.</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-01">
<a name="step_1_2" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-2-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 2" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/e/ee/Write-a-Script-Step-2-Version-3.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-2-Version-3.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="d16096631a091ebacf27616505a8a342" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/e/ee/Write-a-Script-Step-2-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-2-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('d16096631a091ebacf27616505a8a342')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 2" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/e/ee/Write-a-Script-Step-2-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-2-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/e/ee/Write-a-Script-Step-2-Version-3.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-2-Version-3.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="d16096631a091ebacf27616505a8a342"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/e\/ee\/Write-a-Script-Step-2-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-2-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/e\/ee\/Write-a-Script-Step-2-Version-3.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-2-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_1" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_1" class="sv_vote">14</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">2</div><div class="step" id="d07a4e8833f3dbee5ff33dda3504f26f">
<b class="whb">Pick a genre for your story.</b> Genre is an important storytelling device that lets readers know what sort of story to expect. Look at the movies or TV shows that you enjoy most and try to write a script in a similar style.<sup id="_ref-2" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 2"><a href="#_note-2">[2]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden="" id="ts_popup_2" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup>
<ul><li>Combine genres to make something unique. For example, you may have a western movie that takes place in space or a romance movie with horror elements.
</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="green_box mobile">
<p><b>Picking a Genre</b></p>
<p>If you like big set pieces and explosions, consider writing an <b>action</b> film.</p>
<p>If you want to scare other people, try writing a <b>horror</b> script.</p>
<p>If you want to tell a story about a relationship, try writing a <b>drama</b> or <b>romantic comedy</b>.</p>
<p>If you like a lot of special effects or what could happen in the future, write a <b>science fiction</b> film.</p>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="wh_ad_inner w_label al_grey" data-service="adsense" data-slot="4498472735" data-smallheight="250" data-small="1" data-type="step2" data-containerless="1" data-fullwidthadsense="1" data-channels="6049028097" data-mobilechannels="7928712280,6429618073" data-largechannels="2060152247,5763098696" data-smallchannels="8156154280" data-mediumchannels="4066873649" data-observerloading="1" data-sizes-array="0" data-gptdisplaylate="1"><div id="step2_ad_1"></div></div>
<script>WH.ads.addBodyAd('step2_ad_1')</script><div class="al_method">Advertisement</div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-02">
<a name="step_1_3" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-3-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 3" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/5/50/Write-a-Script-Step-3-Version-3.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-3-Version-3.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="ebd8eb2d13e5e8bfa5efe907f28b5a9a" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/5/50/Write-a-Script-Step-3-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-3-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('ebd8eb2d13e5e8bfa5efe907f28b5a9a')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 3" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/5/50/Write-a-Script-Step-3-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-3-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/5/50/Write-a-Script-Step-3-Version-3.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-3-Version-3.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="ebd8eb2d13e5e8bfa5efe907f28b5a9a"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/5\/50\/Write-a-Script-Step-3-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-3-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/5\/50\/Write-a-Script-Step-3-Version-3.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-3-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_2" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_2" class="sv_vote">8</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">3</div><div class="step" id="514434b71ae03c2a37b05f90d7bb3bfa">
<b class="whb">Choose a setting for your script to take place.</b> Make sure the setting works with the story or theme of your script. Make a list of at least 3-4 different settings for your characters to travel between in your script so it stays interesting.<sup id="_ref-3" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 3"><a href="#_note-3">[3]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden="" id="ts_popup_3" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup>
<ul>
<li>For example, if one of your themes is isolation, you may choose to set your script in an abandoned house.</li>
<li>The genre you pick will also help you choose your setting. For example, it's unlikely that you'd set a western story in New York City.</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-03">
<a name="step_1_4" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-4-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 4" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/c/c8/Write-a-Script-Step-4-Version-3.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-4-Version-3.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="a406bd2c359e6d157359ae3dbdb1bd87" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/c/c8/Write-a-Script-Step-4-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-4-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('a406bd2c359e6d157359ae3dbdb1bd87')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 4" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/c/c8/Write-a-Script-Step-4-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-4-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/c/c8/Write-a-Script-Step-4-Version-3.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-4-Version-3.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="a406bd2c359e6d157359ae3dbdb1bd87"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/c\/c8\/Write-a-Script-Step-4-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-4-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/c\/c8\/Write-a-Script-Step-4-Version-3.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-4-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_3" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_3" class="sv_vote">6</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">4</div><div class="step" id="758e158ffb3e2069541c9d4360c93789">
<b class="whb">Make an interesting protagonist.</b> When you're making a protagonist, give them a goal that they are trying to achieve throughout the script. Give your character a flaw, such as being a constant liar or only thinking for themselves, to make them more interesting. By the end of your script, your character should go through an arc and change in some way. Brainstorm who your character is at the beginning of the story versus how the events would change them.<sup id="_ref-4" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 4"><a href="#_note-4">[4]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden="" id="ts_popup_4" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup>
<ul><li>Don't forget to figure out a <a href="/Name-a-Main-Character" title="Name a Main Character">memorable name</a> for your character!</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-04">
<a name="step_1_5" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-5-Version-2.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 5" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/0/0d/Write-a-Script-Step-5-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-5-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="2d33869c532dcb0bae9dca2624cc784a" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/0/0d/Write-a-Script-Step-5-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-5-Version-2.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('2d33869c532dcb0bae9dca2624cc784a')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 5" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/0/0d/Write-a-Script-Step-5-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-5-Version-2.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/0/0d/Write-a-Script-Step-5-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-5-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="2d33869c532dcb0bae9dca2624cc784a"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/0\/0d\/Write-a-Script-Step-5-Version-2.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-5-Version-2.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/0\/0d\/Write-a-Script-Step-5-Version-2.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-5-Version-2.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_4" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_4" class="sv_vote">3</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">5</div><div class="step" id="4b1b1c3263e2c4a0915cd9b516972e55">
<b class="whb">Create an antagonist that opposes your protagonist.</b> The antagonist is the driving force that goes against your protagonist. Give your protagonist and antagonist similar qualities, but change the way the antagonist approaches them. For example, your protagonist may be trying to save the world, but the antagonist may think the only way to save it is to destroy it.<sup id="_ref-5" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 5"><a href="#_note-5">[5]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden="" id="ts_popup_5" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup>
<ul>
<li>If you're writing a horror story, your antagonist may be a monster or a masked killer.</li>
<li>In a romantic comedy, the antagonist is the person your main character is trying to woo.</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-05">
<a name="step_1_6" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-6-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 6" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/9/92/Write-a-Script-Step-6-Version-3.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-6-Version-3.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="b4ff7fad87dcb36b3aad35d8f8afa33b" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/9/92/Write-a-Script-Step-6-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-6-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('b4ff7fad87dcb36b3aad35d8f8afa33b')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 6" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/9/92/Write-a-Script-Step-6-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-6-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/9/92/Write-a-Script-Step-6-Version-3.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-6-Version-3.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="b4ff7fad87dcb36b3aad35d8f8afa33b"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/9\/92\/Write-a-Script-Step-6-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-6-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/9\/92\/Write-a-Script-Step-6-Version-3.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-6-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_5" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_5" class="sv_vote">8</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">6</div><div class="step" id="49c75b92fb6363843025ed224199ae69">
<b class="whb">Write a 1-2 sentence logline to summarize the plot of your script.</b> A logline is a short summary of the main events in your film. Use descriptive language to help your logline sound unique so other people understand what the main ideas of your story are. Make sure the conflict is present in your logline.<sup id="_ref-6" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 6"><a href="#_note-6">[6]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden="" id="ts_popup_6" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup>
<ul><li>For example, if you wanted to write a logline for the movie <i>A Quiet Place</i>, you may say, "A family is attacked by monsters," but it doesn't give any details. Instead, if you wrote, "A family must live in silence to avoid being captured by monsters with ultra-sensitive hearing," then the person reading your logline understands the main points of your script.</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>

<div class="section steps   sticky">
<h3 class="in-block block_header">
<div class="altblock"><div>Part <span>2</span>
</div>
</div>
<span class="mw-headline" id="Outlining-Your-Script"><div class="method_label">Part 2 of 5:</div>Outlining Your Script</span>
</h3>
<div id="steps_3" class="section_text">
<ol class="steps_list_2">
<li id="step-id-16">
<a name="step_2_1" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-7-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 7" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/1/18/Write-a-Script-Step-7-Version-3.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-7-Version-3.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="caed32a6779791f2dcfa72d90ea056a4" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/18/Write-a-Script-Step-7-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-7-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('caed32a6779791f2dcfa72d90ea056a4')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 7" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/18/Write-a-Script-Step-7-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-7-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/1/18/Write-a-Script-Step-7-Version-3.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-7-Version-3.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="caed32a6779791f2dcfa72d90ea056a4"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/1\/18\/Write-a-Script-Step-7-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-7-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/1\/18\/Write-a-Script-Step-7-Version-3.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-7-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_6" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_6" class="sv_vote">4</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">1</div><div class="step" id="b1c3b6af8bf898c2c58e056527abc0fe">
<b class="whb">Brainstorm plot ideas on index cards.</b> Write down each event in your script on their own note cards. This way you can easily reorganize the events to see what works best. Write down all of your ideas, even if you think they're bad, since you may not know what will work best in your final script.
<ul><li>If you don't want to use index cards, you may also use a word document or screenwriting software, such as WriterDuet or Final Draft.</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-17">
<a name="step_2_2" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-8-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 8" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/8/8d/Write-a-Script-Step-8-Version-3.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-8-Version-3.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="181c9f6a3184720874cc72daa70b8e96" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/8/8d/Write-a-Script-Step-8-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-8-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('181c9f6a3184720874cc72daa70b8e96')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 8" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/8/8d/Write-a-Script-Step-8-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-8-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/8/8d/Write-a-Script-Step-8-Version-3.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-8-Version-3.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="181c9f6a3184720874cc72daa70b8e96"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/8\/8d\/Write-a-Script-Step-8-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-8-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/8\/8d\/Write-a-Script-Step-8-Version-3.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-8-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_7" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_7" class="sv_vote">3</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">2</div><div class="step" id="792ea739ea06e6edb52f76023523fbce">
<b class="whb">Arrange the events in the order you want them in your script.</b> Once you write all of your ideas on cards, lay them out on a table or floor and organize them in the chronological order of your story. Look at how certain events lead into one another to see if it makes sense. If it doesn't, set the index cards aside to see if they'd work somewhere better in your outline.<sup id="_ref-7" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 7"><a href="#_note-7">[7]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden="" id="ts_popup_7" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup>
<ul><li>Have events in the future take place early in your film if you want to make a mind-bending movie with twists, such as <i>Inception</i>.
</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="green_box expert mobile">	<div class="green_box_expert_head">EXPERT TIP</div>	<div class="green_box_person expert" data-link="/Author/Melessa-Sargent">			<div class="green_box_expert_dialog">				<div class="green_box_expert_dialog_upper">					<div class="green_box_person_circle"><picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="/images/thumb/c/ce/Melessa_sargent.jpg/-crop-100-100-100px-Melessa_sargent.jpg.webp"><img src="/images/thumb/c/ce/Melessa_sargent.jpg/-crop-100-100-100px-Melessa_sargent.jpg" alt="Melessa Sargent" loading="lazy" width="45" height="45" style="max-width: 45px"></picture></div>					<p>						<a href="/Author/Melessa-Sargent" class="click_out">							Melessa Sargent						</a>					</p>					Professional Writer				</div>				Melessa Sargent is the President of Scriptwriters Network, a non-profit organization that brings in entertainment professionals to teach the art and business of script writing for TV, features and new media. The Network serves its members by providing educational programming, developing access and opportunity through alliances with industry professionals, and furthering the cause and quality of writing in the entertainment industry. Under Melessa's leadership, SWN has won numbers awards including the Los Angeles Award from 2014 through 2021, and the Innovation &amp; Excellence award in 2020.			</div>		<div class="green_box_person_circle"><picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="/images/thumb/c/ce/Melessa_sargent.jpg/-crop-100-100-100px-Melessa_sargent.jpg.webp"><img src="/images/thumb/c/ce/Melessa_sargent.jpg/-crop-100-100-100px-Melessa_sargent.jpg" alt="Melessa Sargent" loading="lazy" width="45" height="45" style="max-width: 45px"></picture></div>		<div class="green_box_expert_info">			<span>Melessa Sargent</span><br>			Professional Writer		</div>	</div>	<div class="green_box_content"><p><b>Also be sure to consider how many acts to include.</b> A TV script should be 5 acts if it's for a commercial network like CBS, NBC, or ABC. A non-commercial script, such as for Netflix or Amazon, should be 3 acts. Feature scripts are also usually 3 acts.</p></div>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-18">
<a name="step_2_3" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-9-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 9" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/b/ba/Write-a-Script-Step-9-Version-3.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-9-Version-3.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="5863b9b3ae0f5e404dbdd543b8bc604f" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/b/ba/Write-a-Script-Step-9-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-9-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('5863b9b3ae0f5e404dbdd543b8bc604f')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 9" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/b/ba/Write-a-Script-Step-9-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-9-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/b/ba/Write-a-Script-Step-9-Version-3.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-9-Version-3.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="5863b9b3ae0f5e404dbdd543b8bc604f"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/b\/ba\/Write-a-Script-Step-9-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-9-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/b\/ba\/Write-a-Script-Step-9-Version-3.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-9-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_8" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_8" class="sv_vote">3</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">3</div><div class="step" id="d178fde09da2d7f38c59d3ce22dcad6d">
<b class="whb">Ask yourself the importance of each scene you want to include.</b> As you go through your outline ask yourself questions, such as, "What is the main point of this scene?" or, "How does this scene move the story forward?" Go through each of the scenes to see if they add to the story or if they're only there to fill out space. If the scene doesn't have a point or move the story, you can probably remove it.<sup id="_ref-8" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 8"><a href="#_note-8">[8]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden="" id="ts_popup_8" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup>
<ul><li>For example, if the scene is your character just shopping for groceries, it doesn't add anything to the story. However, if your character bumps into someone at the grocery store and they hold a conversation related to the main idea of the movie, then you can keep it.
</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="green_box expert mobile">	<div class="green_box_expert_head">EXPERT TIP</div>	<div class="green_box_person expert" data-link="/Author/Melessa-Sargent">			<div class="green_box_expert_dialog">				<div class="green_box_expert_dialog_upper">					<div class="green_box_person_circle"><picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="/images/thumb/c/ce/Melessa_sargent.jpg/-crop-100-100-100px-Melessa_sargent.jpg.webp"><img src="/images/thumb/c/ce/Melessa_sargent.jpg/-crop-100-100-100px-Melessa_sargent.jpg" alt="Melessa Sargent" loading="lazy" width="45" height="45" style="max-width: 45px"></picture></div>					<p>						<a href="/Author/Melessa-Sargent" class="click_out">							Melessa Sargent						</a>					</p>					Professional Writer				</div>				Melessa Sargent is the President of Scriptwriters Network, a non-profit organization that brings in entertainment professionals to teach the art and business of script writing for TV, features and new media. The Network serves its members by providing educational programming, developing access and opportunity through alliances with industry professionals, and furthering the cause and quality of writing in the entertainment industry. Under Melessa's leadership, SWN has won numbers awards including the Los Angeles Award from 2014 through 2021, and the Innovation &amp; Excellence award in 2020.			</div>		<div class="green_box_person_circle"><picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="/images/thumb/c/ce/Melessa_sargent.jpg/-crop-100-100-100px-Melessa_sargent.jpg.webp"><img src="/images/thumb/c/ce/Melessa_sargent.jpg/-crop-100-100-100px-Melessa_sargent.jpg" alt="Melessa Sargent" loading="lazy" width="45" height="45" style="max-width: 45px"></picture></div>		<div class="green_box_expert_info">			<span>Melessa Sargent</span><br>			Professional Writer		</div>	</div>	<div class="green_box_content"><p><b>Consider how many acts should be included.</b> Melessa Sargent, the President of Screenwriters Network, says: "A TV script should be 5 acts if it's for a commercial network like CBS, NBC, or ABC. A non-commercial script, such as for Netflix or Amazon, should be 3 acts. In either case, a teaser is included and is considered the first act. Feature scripts are also usually 3 acts."</p></div>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-19">
<a name="step_2_4" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-10-Version-2.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 10" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/e/eb/Write-a-Script-Step-10-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-10-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="e2f6775a70a6762ef84e49228090e45d" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/e/eb/Write-a-Script-Step-10-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-10-Version-2.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('e2f6775a70a6762ef84e49228090e45d')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 10" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/e/eb/Write-a-Script-Step-10-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-10-Version-2.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/e/eb/Write-a-Script-Step-10-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-10-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="e2f6775a70a6762ef84e49228090e45d"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/e\/eb\/Write-a-Script-Step-10-Version-2.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-10-Version-2.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/e\/eb\/Write-a-Script-Step-10-Version-2.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-10-Version-2.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_9" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_9" class="sv_vote">5</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">4</div><div class="step" id="226b2e087247175e9ab03106808759ca">
<b class="whb">Use high and low moments as your act breaks.</b> Act breaks help separate your story into 3 parts: setup, confrontation, and resolution. The setup, or Act I, begins at the start of your story and ends when your character makes a choice that changes their lives forever. Throughout the confrontation, or Act II, your protagonist will work towards their goal and interact with your antagonist leading up to the climactic point of the story. The resolution, or Act III, takes place after the climax shows what happens afterward.<sup id="_ref-9" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 9"><a href="#_note-9">[9]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden="" id="ts_popup_9" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup>

</div>
<div class="green_box mobile"><p><b>Tip:</b> TV scripts usually hit act breaks when they cut to commercials. Watch shows similar to the story you're writing to see what happens just before they go to a commercial break.</p></div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<div class="wh_ad_inner w_label al_grey dfpsmall dfpsmallmethod containerless_ad fluid" data-service="adsense" data-slot="7710650179" data-width="728" data-height="90" data-smallheight="250" data-type="method" data-small="1" data-channels="6049028097" data-smallservice="dfp" data-adunitpath="/10095428/engl/engl_gam_sma_meth0" data-size="[[300, 250],&quot;fluid&quot;]" data-apsload="1" data-prebidserverload="1" data-prebidload="1" data-aps-timeout="800" data-containerless="1" data-fullwidthadsense="1" data-fluidsize="1" data-mediumchannels="3005955957,4066873649" data-smallchannels="2811805837,8156154280" data-mobilechannels="7928712280,6429618073" data-largechannels="2060152247,5763098696" data-observerloading="1" data-sizes-array="[[300, 250],&quot;fluid&quot;]" data-gptdisplaylate="1"><div id="mobilemethod_ad_2"></div></div>

</ol>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section steps   sticky">
<h3 class="in-block block_header">
<div class="altblock"><div>Part <span>3</span>
</div>
</div>
<span class="mw-headline" id="Formatting-the-Script"><div class="method_label">Part 3 of 5:</div>Formatting the Script</span>
</h3>
<div id="steps_4" class="section_text">
<ol class="steps_list_2">
<li id="step-id-210">
<a name="step_3_1" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-11-Version-2.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 11" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/c/c7/Write-a-Script-Step-11-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-11-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="d172f7a3a157e31ead563efd0c7c1dee" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/c/c7/Write-a-Script-Step-11-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-11-Version-2.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('d172f7a3a157e31ead563efd0c7c1dee')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 11" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/c/c7/Write-a-Script-Step-11-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-11-Version-2.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/c/c7/Write-a-Script-Step-11-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-11-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="d172f7a3a157e31ead563efd0c7c1dee"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/c\/c7\/Write-a-Script-Step-11-Version-2.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-11-Version-2.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/c\/c7\/Write-a-Script-Step-11-Version-2.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-11-Version-2.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_10" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_10" class="sv_vote">6</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">1</div><div class="step" id="ff9e7f103a937b3e2a2bd34bf34a1481">
<b class="whb">Create a title page for your script.</b> Include the title of your script in all caps in the center of the page. Put a line break after the title of your script, then type "written by." Add another line break before typing your name. Leave contact information, such as an email address and phone number in the bottom left margins.<sup id="_ref-10" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 10"><a href="#_note-10">[10]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden="" id="ts_popup_10" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup>
<ul><li>If the script is based on any other stories or films, include a few lines with the phrase "Based on the story by" followed by the names of the original authors.
</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="green_box expert_short mobile">	<div class="green_box_expert_head">EXPERT TIP</div>	<div class="green_box_content"><p>Try scriptwriting software to make formatting your script easy. It can help a lot, especially if you've never written a screenplay before.</p></div>	<div class="green_box_person expert" data-link="/Author/Melessa-Sargent">			<div class="green_box_expert_dialog">				<div class="green_box_expert_dialog_upper">					<div class="green_box_person_circle"><picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="/images/thumb/c/ce/Melessa_sargent.jpg/-crop-100-100-100px-Melessa_sargent.jpg.webp"><img src="/images/thumb/c/ce/Melessa_sargent.jpg/-crop-100-100-100px-Melessa_sargent.jpg" alt="Melessa Sargent" loading="lazy" width="45" height="45" style="max-width: 45px"></picture></div>					<p>Melessa Sargent</p>					Professional Writer				</div>				Melessa Sargent is the President of Scriptwriters Network, a non-profit organization that brings in entertainment professionals to teach the art and business of script writing for TV, features and new media. The Network serves its members by providing educational programming, developing access and opportunity through alliances with industry professionals, and furthering the cause and quality of writing in the entertainment industry. Under Melessa's leadership, SWN has won numbers awards including the Los Angeles Award from 2014 through 2021, and the Innovation &amp; Excellence award in 2020.			</div>		<div class="green_box_person_circle"><picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="/images/thumb/c/ce/Melessa_sargent.jpg/-crop-100-100-100px-Melessa_sargent.jpg.webp"><img src="/images/thumb/c/ce/Melessa_sargent.jpg/-crop-100-100-100px-Melessa_sargent.jpg" alt="Melessa Sargent" loading="lazy" width="45" height="45" style="max-width: 45px"></picture></div>		<div class="green_box_expert_info">
<b>Melessa Sargent</b><br>Professional Writer</div>	</div>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-211">
<a name="step_3_2" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-12-Version-2.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 12" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/5/52/Write-a-Script-Step-12-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-12-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="1f5bc6e174f2134be0aee74945557053" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/5/52/Write-a-Script-Step-12-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-12-Version-2.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('1f5bc6e174f2134be0aee74945557053')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 12" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/5/52/Write-a-Script-Step-12-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-12-Version-2.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/5/52/Write-a-Script-Step-12-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-12-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="1f5bc6e174f2134be0aee74945557053"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/5\/52\/Write-a-Script-Step-12-Version-2.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-12-Version-2.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/5\/52\/Write-a-Script-Step-12-Version-2.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-12-Version-2.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_11" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_11" class="sv_vote">2</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">2</div><div class="step" id="1db8bd52b845854280df65251411d137">
<b class="whb">Use size 12 Courier font throughout your whole script.</b> Screenwriting standard is any variation of Courier so it's easy to read. Make sure to use 12-point font since it's what other scripts use and is considered industry standard.<sup id="_ref-11" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 11"><a href="#_note-11">[11]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden="" id="ts_popup_11" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup>
<ul><li>Use any additional formatting, such as bolding or underlining, sparingly since it can distract your reader.
</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="green_box mobile"><p><b>Tip:</b> Screenwriting software, like Celtx, Final Draft, or WriterDuet, all automatically format your script for you so you don't need to worry about changing any settings.</p></div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-212">
<a name="step_3_3" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-13-Version-2.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 13" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/1/19/Write-a-Script-Step-13-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-13-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="f3ac7406dd92a1854d8ce46c74166222" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/19/Write-a-Script-Step-13-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-13-Version-2.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('f3ac7406dd92a1854d8ce46c74166222')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 13" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/19/Write-a-Script-Step-13-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-13-Version-2.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/1/19/Write-a-Script-Step-13-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-13-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="f3ac7406dd92a1854d8ce46c74166222"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/1\/19\/Write-a-Script-Step-13-Version-2.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-13-Version-2.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/1\/19\/Write-a-Script-Step-13-Version-2.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-13-Version-2.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_12" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_12" class="sv_vote">7</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">3</div><div class="step" id="53fe6e21df5792e96d2ad99791bd32c0">
<b class="whb">Put in scene headings whenever you go to a different location.</b> Scene heading should be aligned to the left margin <span class="frac nowrap">1<span class="visualhide">&nbsp;</span><sup>1</sup>⁄<sub>2</sub></span>&nbsp;in (3.8&nbsp;cm) from the edge of the page. Type the scene headings in all caps so they're easily recognizable. Include INT. or EXT. to tell readers if the scene takes place inside or outside. Then, name the specific location followed by the time of day it takes place.<sup id="_ref-12" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 12"><a href="#_note-12">[12]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden="" id="ts_popup_12" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup>
<ul>
<li>For example, a scene heading may read: INT. CLASSROOM - DAY.</li>
<li>Keep scene headings on a single line so they aren't too overwhelming.</li>
<li>If you want to specify a room in a specific location, you can also type scene headings like: INT. JOHN'S HOUSE - KITCHEN - DAY.</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-213">
<a name="step_3_4" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-14-Version-2.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 14" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/7/71/Write-a-Script-Step-14-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-14-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="38de43957b08777b7b560c06c32f0d40" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/71/Write-a-Script-Step-14-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-14-Version-2.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('38de43957b08777b7b560c06c32f0d40')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 14" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/71/Write-a-Script-Step-14-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-14-Version-2.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/7/71/Write-a-Script-Step-14-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-14-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="38de43957b08777b7b560c06c32f0d40"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/7\/71\/Write-a-Script-Step-14-Version-2.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-14-Version-2.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/7\/71\/Write-a-Script-Step-14-Version-2.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-14-Version-2.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_13" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_13" class="sv_vote">7</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">4</div><div class="step" id="9de7f2d2b86e96f74009f53b05cbadb6">
<b class="whb">Write action blocks to describe settings and character actions.</b> Action blocks should be aligned with the left margin and are written in regular sentence structure. Use action lines to denote what a character does and to give brief descriptions about what's happening. Keep action lines brief so they don't overwhelm a reader looking at the page.<sup id="_ref-13" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 13"><a href="#_note-13">[13]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden="" id="ts_popup_13" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup>
<ul>
<li>Avoid writing what the characters are thinking. A good rule of thumb to think about is if it can't be seen on a screen, don't include it in your action block. So instead of saying, "John thinks about pulling the lever but he's not sure if he should," you may write something like, "John's hand twitches near the lever. He grits his teeth and furrows his brow."</li>
<li>When you introduce a character for the first time in an action block, use all caps for their name. Every time after you mention the character name, write it as normal.</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-214">
<a name="step_3_5" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-15-Version-2.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 15" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/e/e1/Write-a-Script-Step-15-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-15-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="ee0342d5095fb4410789ad242cbea223" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/e/e1/Write-a-Script-Step-15-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-15-Version-2.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('ee0342d5095fb4410789ad242cbea223')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 15" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/e/e1/Write-a-Script-Step-15-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-15-Version-2.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/e/e1/Write-a-Script-Step-15-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-15-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="ee0342d5095fb4410789ad242cbea223"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/e\/e1\/Write-a-Script-Step-15-Version-2.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-15-Version-2.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/e\/e1\/Write-a-Script-Step-15-Version-2.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-15-Version-2.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_14" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_14" class="sv_vote">2</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">5</div><div class="step" id="7848874478ec9336aed7aadc049af2ae">
<b class="whb">Center character names and dialogue whenever a character speaks.</b> When a character is about to speak, make sure the margin is set to 3.7&nbsp;in (9.4&nbsp;cm) from the left side of the page. Put the characters name in all caps so a reader or actor can easily see when their lines occur. When you write the dialogue, make sure it's <span class="frac nowrap">2<span class="visualhide">&nbsp;</span><sup>1</sup>⁄<sub>2</sub></span>&nbsp;in (6.4&nbsp;cm) from the left side of the page.<sup id="_ref-14" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 14"><a href="#_note-14">[14]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden="" id="ts_popup_14" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup>
<ul><li>If you want to make it clear how your character is feeling, include a parenthetical on the line right after the character name with an emotion. For example, it may read (excited) or (tense). Make sure the parenthetical is 3.1&nbsp;in (7.9&nbsp;cm) from the left side of the page.</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<div class="wh_ad_inner w_label al_grey dfpsmall dfpsmallmethod containerless_ad fluid" data-service="adsense" data-slot="7710650179" data-width="728" data-height="90" data-smallheight="250" data-type="method" data-small="1" data-channels="6049028097" data-smallservice="dfp" data-adunitpath="/10095428/engl/engl_gam_sma_meth0" data-size="[[300, 250],&quot;fluid&quot;]" data-apsload="1" data-prebidserverload="1" data-prebidload="1" data-aps-timeout="800" data-containerless="1" data-fullwidthadsense="1" data-fluidsize="1" data-mediumchannels="3005955957,4066873649" data-smallchannels="2811805837,8156154280" data-mobilechannels="7928712280,6429618073" data-largechannels="2060152247,5763098696" data-observerloading="1" data-sizes-array="[[300, 250],&quot;fluid&quot;]" data-gptdisplaylate="1"><div id="mobilemethod_ad_3"></div></div>

</ol>

<div class="section steps   sticky">
<h3 class="in-block block_header">
<div class="altblock"><div>Part <span>4</span>
</div>
</div>
<span class="mw-headline" id="Writing-Your-First-Draft"><div class="method_label">Part 4 of 5:</div>Writing Your First Draft</span>
</h3>
<div id="steps_5" class="section_text">
<ol class="steps_list_2">
<li id="step-id-315">
<a name="step_4_1" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-16-Version-2.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 16" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/e/ef/Write-a-Script-Step-16-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-16-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="c5b602150e6df57ed9cf324441624616" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/e/ef/Write-a-Script-Step-16-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-16-Version-2.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('c5b602150e6df57ed9cf324441624616')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 16" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/e/ef/Write-a-Script-Step-16-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-16-Version-2.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/e/ef/Write-a-Script-Step-16-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-16-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="c5b602150e6df57ed9cf324441624616"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/e\/ef\/Write-a-Script-Step-16-Version-2.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-16-Version-2.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/e\/ef\/Write-a-Script-Step-16-Version-2.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-16-Version-2.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_15" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_15" class="sv_vote">1</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">1</div><div class="step" id="ba0bb7e3c5abc5cb2fa53f6a958a8541">
<b class="whb">Set a deadline so you have a goal to reach.</b> Choose a date that's about 8-12 weeks away from when you start since these are the usual industry times that writers have to work on a script. Mark the deadline on a calendar or as a reminder on your phone so it holds you accountable for working on your script.<sup id="_ref-15" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 15"><a href="#_note-15">[15]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden="" id="ts_popup_15" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup>
<ul><li>Tell others about your goal and ask them to hold you accountable for finishing your work.</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-316">
<a name="step_4_2" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-17-Version-2.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 17" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/8/81/Write-a-Script-Step-17-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-17-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="6812541aa260002a88bf6d02055a05f0" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/8/81/Write-a-Script-Step-17-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-17-Version-2.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('6812541aa260002a88bf6d02055a05f0')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 17" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/8/81/Write-a-Script-Step-17-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-17-Version-2.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/8/81/Write-a-Script-Step-17-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-17-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="6812541aa260002a88bf6d02055a05f0"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/8\/81\/Write-a-Script-Step-17-Version-2.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-17-Version-2.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/8\/81\/Write-a-Script-Step-17-Version-2.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-17-Version-2.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_16" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_16" class="sv_vote">2</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">2</div><div class="step" id="cc4412c342d26aa8b8d0062a2e2d32e4">
<b class="whb">Plan to write at least 1-2 pages per day.</b> During your first draft, just write the ideas that come to your head and follow along with your outline. Don't worry about spelling or grammar entirely since you just need to get your story written down. If you aim to do 1-2 pages each day, you'll finish your first draft within 60-90 days. 
<ul>
<li>Choose a set time each day to sit down and write so you don't get distracted.</li>
<li>Turn off your phone or internet connection so you can just focus on writing.
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="green_box expert_short mobile">	<div class="green_box_expert_head">EXPERT TIP</div>	<div class="green_box_content"><p>"Feature scripts should be between 95-110 pages. TV scripts should be 30-35 pages for a half-hour show or 60-65 pages for a 1 hour show."</p></div>	<div class="green_box_person expert" data-link="/Author/Melessa-Sargent">			<div class="green_box_expert_dialog">				<div class="green_box_expert_dialog_upper">					<div class="green_box_person_circle"><picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="/images/thumb/c/ce/Melessa_sargent.jpg/-crop-100-100-100px-Melessa_sargent.jpg.webp"><img src="/images/thumb/c/ce/Melessa_sargent.jpg/-crop-100-100-100px-Melessa_sargent.jpg" alt="Melessa Sargent" loading="lazy" width="45" height="45" style="max-width: 45px"></picture></div>					<p>Melessa Sargent</p>					Professional Writer				</div>				Melessa Sargent is the President of Scriptwriters Network, a non-profit organization that brings in entertainment professionals to teach the art and business of script writing for TV, features and new media. The Network serves its members by providing educational programming, developing access and opportunity through alliances with industry professionals, and furthering the cause and quality of writing in the entertainment industry. Under Melessa's leadership, SWN has won numbers awards including the Los Angeles Award from 2014 through 2021, and the Innovation &amp; Excellence award in 2020.			</div>		<div class="green_box_person_circle"><picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="/images/thumb/c/ce/Melessa_sargent.jpg/-crop-100-100-100px-Melessa_sargent.jpg.webp"><img src="/images/thumb/c/ce/Melessa_sargent.jpg/-crop-100-100-100px-Melessa_sargent.jpg" alt="Melessa Sargent" loading="lazy" width="45" height="45" style="max-width: 45px"></picture></div>		<div class="green_box_expert_info">

</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-317">
<a name="step_4_3" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-18-Version-2.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 18" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/a/ab/Write-a-Script-Step-18-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-18-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="e8b8b7d0dc149bf3ce2b032f97e6862b" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/a/ab/Write-a-Script-Step-18-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-18-Version-2.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('e8b8b7d0dc149bf3ce2b032f97e6862b')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 18" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/a/ab/Write-a-Script-Step-18-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-18-Version-2.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/a/ab/Write-a-Script-Step-18-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-18-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="e8b8b7d0dc149bf3ce2b032f97e6862b"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/a\/ab\/Write-a-Script-Step-18-Version-2.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-18-Version-2.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/a\/ab\/Write-a-Script-Step-18-Version-2.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-18-Version-2.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_17" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_17" class="sv_vote">1</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">3</div><div class="step" id="46cb317bea7708d15c6fc4e5b1b7a7fa">
<b class="whb">Say your dialogue out loud to see if it sounds natural.</b> As you write what your characters are saying, talk through it out loud. Make sure it flows well and doesn't sound confusing. If you notice any problem areas, highlight or underline the phrases and come back to them next time you edit.<sup id="_ref-16" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 16"><a href="#_note-16">[16]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden="" id="ts_popup_16" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup>
<ul><li>Make sure each character sounds different and has a unique voice. Otherwise, a reader will have a hard time distinguishing between who's speaking.</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-318">
<a name="step_4_4" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-19-Version-2.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 19" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/a/ab/Write-a-Script-Step-19-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-19-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="f25da773216f46733bd2661f255f8b21" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/a/ab/Write-a-Script-Step-19-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-19-Version-2.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('f25da773216f46733bd2661f255f8b21')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 19" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/a/ab/Write-a-Script-Step-19-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-19-Version-2.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/a/ab/Write-a-Script-Step-19-Version-2.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-19-Version-2.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="f25da773216f46733bd2661f255f8b21"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/a\/ab\/Write-a-Script-Step-19-Version-2.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-19-Version-2.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/a\/ab\/Write-a-Script-Step-19-Version-2.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-19-Version-2.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_18" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_18" class="sv_vote">3</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">4</div><div class="step" id="49daeb7eaf070366c7826a6e313c6083">
<b class="whb">Keep writing until you're between 90-120 pages.</b> Think of each page equalling 1 minute of screen time. To write a standard film script, aim to write something about 90-120 pages long so it would run for 1 ½-2 hours long.
<ul>
<li>If you're writing a TV script, aim for 30-40 pages for a half-hour sitcom and 60-70 pages for an hour-long drama.</li>
<li>Short films should be about 10 pages or less.</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<div class="wh_ad_inner w_label al_grey dfpsmall dfpsmallmethod containerless_ad fluid" data-service="adsense" data-slot="7710650179" data-width="728" data-height="90" data-smallheight="250" data-type="method" data-small="1" data-channels="6049028097" data-smallservice="dfp" data-adunitpath="/10095428/engl/engl_gam_sma_meth0" data-size="[[300, 250],&quot;fluid&quot;]" data-apsload="1" data-prebidserverload="1" data-prebidload="1" data-aps-timeout="800" data-containerless="1" data-fullwidthadsense="1" data-fluidsize="1" data-mediumchannels="3005955957,4066873649" data-smallchannels="2811805837,8156154280" data-mobilechannels="7928712280,6429618073" data-largechannels="2060152247,5763098696" data-observerloading="1" data-sizes-array="[[300, 250],&quot;fluid&quot;]" data-gptdisplaylate="1"><div id="mobilemethod_ad_4"></div></div>
