<div class="section steps   sticky">
<h3 class="in-block block_header">
<div class="altblock"><div>Part <span>5</span>
</div>
</div>
<span class="mw-headline" id="Revising-Your-Script"><div class="method_label">Part 5 of 5:</div>Revising Your Script</span>
</h3>
<div id="steps_6" class="section_text">
<ol class="steps_list_2">
<li id="step-id-419">
<a name="step_5_1" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-20.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 20" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/9/99/Write-a-Script-Step-20.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-20.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="1dfc3a86a375008d50e084b29f621b47" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/9/99/Write-a-Script-Step-20.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-20.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('1dfc3a86a375008d50e084b29f621b47')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 20" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/9/99/Write-a-Script-Step-20.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-20.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/9/99/Write-a-Script-Step-20.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-20.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="1dfc3a86a375008d50e084b29f621b47"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/9\/99\/Write-a-Script-Step-20.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-20.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/9\/99\/Write-a-Script-Step-20.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-20.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_19" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_19" class="sv_vote">0</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">1</div><div class="step" id="ac7d2a13bacb8b91411092872ad42b57">
<b class="whb">Take a 1-2 week break from your script when you finish it.</b> Since you've been working on your script for a long period of time, save the file and focus on something else for a few weeks. That way, when you come back to edit it, you'll be able to look at it with fresh eyes.<sup id="_ref-17" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 17"><a href="#_note-17">[17]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden="" id="ts_popup_17" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup>
<ul><li>Start work on another script while you wait if you want to keep working on other ideas.</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-420">
<a name="step_5_2" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-21.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 21" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/3/3f/Write-a-Script-Step-21.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-21.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="f23f5e3826523791cdff6b47c666e421" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/3f/Write-a-Script-Step-21.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-21.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('f23f5e3826523791cdff6b47c666e421')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 21" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/3f/Write-a-Script-Step-21.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-21.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/3/3f/Write-a-Script-Step-21.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-21.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="f23f5e3826523791cdff6b47c666e421"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/3\/3f\/Write-a-Script-Step-21.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-21.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/3\/3f\/Write-a-Script-Step-21.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-21.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_20" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_20" class="sv_vote">2</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">2</div><div class="step" id="0171bbad999d590202da8755887f035c">
<b class="whb">Reread your entire script and take notes on what doesn't make sense.</b> Open your script and read it from start to end. Look for places where the story is the confusing or where characters are doing things without moving the story forward. Write your notes down by hand so you can remember them better.<sup id="_ref-18" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 18"><a href="#_note-18">[18]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden="" id="ts_popup_18" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup>
<ul><li>Try to read your script out loud and don't be afraid to act out parts based on how you think they should be performed. That way, you can catch dialogue or wording that doesn't work as well.
</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="green_box mobile"><p><b>Tip:</b> If you can, print out your screenplay so you can directly write on it.</p></div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-421">
<a name="step_5_3" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-22.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 22" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/3/3a/Write-a-Script-Step-22.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-22.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="fa9d6a1e803535909c9168b3f9a745f0" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/3a/Write-a-Script-Step-22.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-22.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('fa9d6a1e803535909c9168b3f9a745f0')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 22" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/3a/Write-a-Script-Step-22.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-22.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/3/3a/Write-a-Script-Step-22.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-22.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="fa9d6a1e803535909c9168b3f9a745f0"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/3\/3a\/Write-a-Script-Step-22.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-22.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/3\/3a\/Write-a-Script-Step-22.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-22.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_21" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_21" class="sv_vote">3</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">3</div><div class="step" id="ff5f0a98b9ef65b8e8511e2e0c6b72cd">
<b class="whb">Share your script with someone you trust so they can look over it.</b> Ask a friend or parent to look over your script to see what they think. Tell them what sort of feedback you're looking for so they know what to focus on. Ask them questions when they're finished about whether parts make sense or not.<sup id="_ref-19" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 19"><a href="#_note-19">[19]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden="" id="ts_popup_19" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>
<li class="final_li" id="step-id-422">
<a name="step_5_4" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/Image:Write-a-Script-Step-23.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer" style="padding-top:75%">
<img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 23" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/7/7a/Write-a-Script-Step-23.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-23.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="23f02a1b4d7de967f662c8c1112bda57" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7a/Write-a-Script-Step-23.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-23.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('23f02a1b4d7de967f662c8c1112bda57')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Image titled Write a Script Step 23" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7a/Write-a-Script-Step-23.jpg/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-23.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="/images/thumb/7/7a/Write-a-Script-Step-23.jpg/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-23.jpg" data-width="460" data-height="345" id="23f02a1b4d7de967f662c8c1112bda57"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/7\/7a\/Write-a-Script-Step-23.jpg\/v4-460px-Write-a-Script-Step-23.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/7\/7a\/Write-a-Script-Step-23.jpg\/aid3590-v4-728px-Write-a-Script-Step-23.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;p&gt;License: &lt;a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/creativecommons.org\/licenses\/by-nc-sa\/3.0\/\"&gt;Creative Commons&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;\n&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_voting disabled">

	<div class="step_voting_like">
		<a id="sv_vote_button_22" class="sv_heart" href="#"></a>
		<span id="sv_votes_22" class="sv_vote">2</span>
	</div>

</div>
<div class="step_num">4</div><div class="step" id="bab1cb7a9f33b6aa078debdb91a67769">
<b class="whb">Keep rewriting the script until you're happy with it.</b> Work on story and character revisions first to fix larger problems in your script. As you work through each revision, work from larger problems, such as dialogue or confusing action sequences, to minor problems, such as grammar and spelling.
<ul>
<li>Start each draft in a new document so you can cut and paste parts you like from your old script into the new one.</li>
<li>Don't get too nit-picky with yourself or you'll never finish the script you're working on.</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1"></div>
</li>

			Community Q&amp;A
		</span>
	</h2>
	<div id="qa" class="section_text">
		<div id="qa_answered_questions_container">
			<div id="qa_aq_search_container">
				<div id="qa_aq_search_heading" class="qa_section_heading">Search</div>
				<input class="qa_aq_search" placeholder="Type your query here">

			<a id="qa_add_curated_question">Add New Question</a>
			<ul id="qa_article_questions" class="qa_questions qa_aqs qa_waittheresmore">
<li id="qa_question_0" class="qa_aq qa_block " data-aqid="738057" data-cqid="738074" data-caid="738930" data-sqid="" data-qa_inactive="0" data-votes_up="4" data-votes_down="0" data-verifier_id="161074" data-submitter_id="0">
					<div class="qa_divider"></div>
				
					<div class="qa_li_container">
						<div class="qa_question_tab">Question</div>
						<div class="qa_q_txt">How do I start writing a script?</div>
						
				
				
						<div class="qa_answers">
							<div class="qa_expert_area">
								<div class="qa_badge"></div>
				
								<div class="qa_user_hover hint_box">
										<a href="/Author/Melessa-Sargent" class="sp_namelink qa_person_circle" target="_blank">
	<picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="/images/thumb/c/ce/Melessa_sargent.jpg/-crop-149-149-149px-Melessa_sargent.jpg.webp"><img src="/images/thumb/c/ce/Melessa_sargent.jpg/-crop-149-149-149px-Melessa_sargent.jpg" alt="Melessa Sargent" loading="lazy" width="52" height="52" style="max-width: 52px"></picture></a>

<div class="qa_expert_name">
	<a href="/Author/Melessa-Sargent" class="sp_namelink click_out" target="_blank">
		Melessa Sargent
	</a>


	<br>

	Professional Writer
</div>
Melessa Sargent is the President of Scriptwriters Network, a non-profit organization that brings in entertainment professionals to teach the art and business of script writing for TV, features and new media. The Network serves its members by providing educational programming, developing access and opportunity through alliances with industry professionals, and furthering the cause and quality of writing in the entertainment industry. Under Melessa's leadership, SWN has won numbers awards including the Los Angeles Award from 2014 through 2021, and the Innovation &amp; Excellence award in 2020.

										
								</div>
				
									<a href="/Author/Melessa-Sargent" class="sp_namelink qa_person_circle" target="_blank"><picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="/images/thumb/c/ce/Melessa_sargent.jpg/-crop-149-149-149px-Melessa_sargent.jpg.webp"><img src="/images/thumb/c/ce/Melessa_sargent.jpg/-crop-149-149-149px-Melessa_sargent.jpg" alt="Melessa Sargent" loading="lazy" width="52" height="52" style="max-width: 52px"></picture></a>
				
				
								<div class="qa_answerer_info">
									<div class="qa_user_name">
										<a href="/Author/Melessa-Sargent" target="_blank">Melessa Sargent</a>
									</div>
									<div class="qa_user_title">Professional Writer</div>
				
				
									<div class="qa_user_label">Expert Answer</div>
									
								</div>
							</div>
				
							<div class="qa_answer answer ">
								Everything starts with an idea. Make sure you know what your idea is, what you want to write about. Have a character and focus on what the character is going to do. Then take your idea and write it down, from beginning to the end. Let it be just a few pages. Include locations, details, and everything that is on your mind; put the paragraphs. When you actually start to write a script, you would cover everything you have written on these pages, and they will help you to know how you want your story to flow. 
							</div>
								<div class="qa_answer_footer">
									<div class="wh_vote_container qa_vote_buttons">
	<span class="wh_thumb_response wh_thumb_msg">Thanks!</span>

	</div>
</div>



								</div>
						</div>
					</div>
				</li>
					<li id="qa_question_1" class="qa_aq qa_block " data-aqid="542988" data-cqid="543005" data-caid="543861" data-sqid="420316" data-qa_inactive="0" data-votes_up="25" data-votes_down="2" data-verifier_id="0" data-submitter_id="4774693">
					<div class="qa_divider"></div>
				
					<div class="qa_li_container">
						<div class="qa_question_tab">Question</div>
						<div class="qa_q_txt">What is a good script writing software to download? Preferably free.</div>
						
				
				
						<div class="qa_answers">
							<div class="qa_staff_area">
								<div class="qa_badge"></div>
				
								<div class="qa_user_hover hint_box">
										
										<div class="qa_person_circle">
	<picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7c/WHInitials.png/-crop-100-100-100px-WHInitials.png.webp"><img src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7c/WHInitials.png/-crop-100-100-100px-WHInitials.png" width="52" height="52" style="max-width:52px" loading="lazy" alt="wikiHow Staff Editor"></picture>

							<div class="qa_answer answer ">
								Websites and software such as WriterDuet and Celtx are great programs that are free to use with the option to upgrade. If you want to try paid screenwriting software, Final Draft and Fade In have free trials you can use.

					<li id="qa_question_2" class="qa_aq qa_block " data-aqid="543369" data-cqid="543386" data-caid="544242" data-sqid="2108013" data-qa_inactive="0" data-votes_up="34" data-votes_down="6" data-verifier_id="0" data-submitter_id="4774693">
					<div class="qa_divider"></div>
				
					<div class="qa_li_container">
						<div class="qa_question_tab">Question</div>
						<div class="qa_q_txt">What is the length of a TV pilot script (not the duration of the actual program)</div>
						
				
				
						<div class="qa_answers">
							<div class="qa_staff_area">
								<div class="qa_badge"></div>
				
								<div class="qa_user_hover hint_box">
										
										<div class="qa_person_circle">
	<picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7c/WHInitials.png/-crop-100-100-100px-WHInitials.png.webp"><img src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7c/WHInitials.png/-crop-100-100-100px-WHInitials.png" width="52" height="52" style="max-width:52px" loading="lazy" alt="wikiHow Staff Editor"></picture>

<div class="qa_ta_name">
	<a href="/wikiHow:Content-Management" class="sp_namelink click_out" target="_blank">wikiHow Staff Editor</a><br>
	Staff Answer
</div>

This answer was written by one of our trained team of researchers who validated it for accuracy and comprehensiveness.
								</div>
				
				
								<div class="qa_person_circle">
									<picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7c/WHInitials.png/-crop-100-100-100px-WHInitials.png.webp"><img src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7c/WHInitials.png/-crop-100-100-100px-WHInitials.png" width="52" height="52" style="max-width:52px" loading="lazy" alt="wikiHow Staff Editor"></picture>

								<div class="qa_answerer_info">
				
									<div class="qa_user_name">wikiHow Staff Editor</div>
				
									<div class="qa_user_label">Staff Answer</div>
									
								</div>
							</div>
				
							<div class="qa_answer answer ">
								TV pilots are usually around 30-35 pages for a 30-minute show and 60-70 pages for a 60-minute show.

					<div class="qa_divider"></div>
				
					<div class="qa_li_container">
						<div class="qa_question_tab">Question</div>
						<div class="qa_q_txt">What is a good way to start off a scene? </div>
						
				
				
						<div class="qa_answers">
							<div class="qa_staff_area">
								<div class="qa_badge"></div>
				
								<div class="qa_user_hover hint_box">
										
										<div class="qa_person_circle">
	<picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7c/WHInitials.png/-crop-100-100-100px-WHInitials.png.webp"><img src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7c/WHInitials.png/-crop-100-100-100px-WHInitials.png" width="52" height="52" style="max-width:52px" loading="lazy" alt="wikiHow Staff Editor"></picture>

<div class="qa_ta_name">
	<a href="/wikiHow:Content-Management" class="sp_namelink click_out" target="_blank">wikiHow Staff Editor</a><br>
	Staff Answer
</div>

This answer was written by one of our trained team of researchers who validated it for accuracy and comprehensiveness.
								</div>
				
				
								<div class="qa_person_circle">
									<picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7c/WHInitials.png/-crop-100-100-100px-WHInitials.png.webp"><img src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7c/WHInitials.png/-crop-100-100-100px-WHInitials.png" width="52" height="52" style="max-width:52px" loading="lazy" alt="wikiHow Staff Editor"></picture>
</div>
				
								<div class="qa_answerer_info">
				
									<div class="qa_user_name">wikiHow Staff Editor</div>
				
									<div class="qa_user_label">Staff Answer</div>
									
								</div>
							</div>
				
							<div class="qa_answer answer ">
								Usually with 2-3 lines of action or simple scene description work best when you're starting a new scene.
							</div>
								<div class="qa_answer_footer">

					<li id="qa_question_4" class="qa_aq qa_block " data-aqid="542995" data-cqid="543012" data-caid="543868" data-sqid="1000701" data-qa_inactive="0" data-votes_up="13" data-votes_down="3" data-verifier_id="0" data-submitter_id="4774693">
					<div class="qa_divider"></div>
				
					<div class="qa_li_container">
						<div class="qa_question_tab">Question</div>
						<div class="qa_q_txt">What the difference between documentary script format or commercial movies scripts?</div>
						
				
				
						<div class="qa_answers">
							<div class="qa_staff_area">
								<div class="qa_badge"></div>
				
								<div class="qa_user_hover hint_box">
										
										<div class="qa_person_circle">
	<picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7c/WHInitials.png/-crop-100-100-100px-WHInitials.png.webp"><img src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7c/WHInitials.png/-crop-100-100-100px-WHInitials.png" width="52" height="52" style="max-width:52px" loading="lazy" alt="wikiHow Staff Editor"></picture>

<div class="qa_ta_name">
	<a href="/wikiHow:Content-Management" class="sp_namelink click_out" target="_blank">wikiHow Staff Editor</a><br>
	Staff Answer
</div>

This answer was written by one of our trained team of researchers who validated it for accuracy and comprehensiveness.
								</div>
				
				
								<div class="qa_person_circle">
									<picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7c/WHInitials.png/-crop-100-100-100px-WHInitials.png.webp"><img src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7c/WHInitials.png/-crop-100-100-100px-WHInitials.png" width="52" height="52" style="max-width:52px" loading="lazy" alt="wikiHow Staff Editor"></picture>

								<div class="qa_answerer_info">
				
									<div class="qa_user_name">wikiHow Staff Editor</div>
				
									<div class="qa_user_label">Staff Answer</div>
									
								</div>
							</div>
				
							<div class="qa_answer answer ">
								Documentary scripts lay out what types of shots to get, such as nature footage or specific interviews. You can't plan for what an interviewee may say in a documentary, but you can plan out specific questions to help guide them toward the answers you want.
							</div>

					<li id="qa_question_5" class="qa_aq qa_block " data-aqid="542990" data-cqid="543007" data-caid="543863" data-sqid="840798" data-qa_inactive="0" data-votes_up="18" data-votes_down="3" data-verifier_id="0" data-submitter_id="4774693">
					<div class="qa_divider"></div>
				
					<div class="qa_li_container">
						<div class="qa_question_tab">Question</div>
						<div class="qa_q_txt">Is there any matter of light and camera in film script?</div>
						
				
				
						<div class="qa_answers">
							<div class="qa_staff_area">
								<div class="qa_badge"></div>
				
								<div class="qa_user_hover hint_box">
										
										<div class="qa_person_circle">
	<picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7c/WHInitials.png/-crop-100-100-100px-WHInitials.png.webp"><img src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7c/WHInitials.png/-crop-100-100-100px-WHInitials.png" width="52" height="52" style="max-width:52px" loading="lazy" alt="wikiHow Staff Editor"></picture>

<div class="qa_ta_name">
	<a href="/wikiHow:Content-Management" class="sp_namelink click_out" target="_blank">wikiHow Staff Editor</a><br>
	Staff Answer
</div>

This answer was written by one of our trained team of researchers who validated it for accuracy and comprehensiveness.
								</div>
				
				
								<div class="qa_person_circle">
									<picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7c/WHInitials.png/-crop-100-100-100px-WHInitials.png.webp"><img src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7c/WHInitials.png/-crop-100-100-100px-WHInitials.png" width="52" height="52" style="max-width:52px" loading="lazy" alt="wikiHow Staff Editor"></picture>

								<div class="qa_answerer_info">
				
									<div class="qa_user_name">wikiHow Staff Editor</div>
				
									<div class="qa_user_label">Staff Answer</div>
									
								</div>
							</div>
				
							<div class="qa_answer answer ">
								Usually, camera movements and lighting are used sparingly in a film script since that's the job of the director and director of photography on a film set.
							</div>

					<li id="qa_question_6" class="qa_aq qa_block " data-aqid="80809" data-cqid="80826" data-caid="81682" data-sqid="653238" data-qa_inactive="0" data-votes_up="144" data-votes_down="23" data-verifier_id="0" data-submitter_id="0">
					<div class="qa_divider"></div>
				
					<div class="qa_li_container">
						<div class="qa_question_tab">Question</div>
						<div class="qa_q_txt">How do I write about the characters in the script?</div>
						
				
				
						<div class="qa_answers">
							<div class="qa_user_area">
								
				
								<div class="qa_user_hover hint_box">
										
										
								</div>
				
				
								<div class="qa_person_circle">
									<picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="/images/thumb/b/b0/CommunityAvatar2.png/-crop-104-104-104px-CommunityAvatar2.png.webp"><img src="/images/thumb/b/b0/CommunityAvatar2.png/-crop-104-104-104px-CommunityAvatar2.png" width="52" height="52" style="max-width:52px" loading="lazy" alt="Community Answer"></picture>

									<div class="qa_user_label">Community Answer</div>
									
								</div>
							</div>
				
							<div class="qa_answer answer ">
								Give brief descriptions of your characters in the script but try to show instead of tell - you want the characters' actions to explain what kind of people they are.

					<li id="qa_question_7" class="qa_aq qa_block " data-aqid="37284" data-cqid="37301" data-caid="38157" data-sqid="259251" data-qa_inactive="0" data-votes_up="173" data-votes_down="28" data-verifier_id="0" data-submitter_id="0">
					<div class="qa_divider"></div>
				
					<div class="qa_li_container">
						<div class="qa_question_tab">Question</div>
						<div class="qa_q_txt">Where can I see sample scripts?</div>
						
				
				
						<div class="qa_answers">
							<div class="qa_user_area">
								
				
								<div class="qa_user_hover hint_box">
										
										
								</div>
				
				
								<div class="qa_person_circle">
									<picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="/images/thumb/b/b0/CommunityAvatar2.png/-crop-104-104-104px-CommunityAvatar2.png.webp"><img src="/images/thumb/b/b0/CommunityAvatar2.png/-crop-104-104-104px-CommunityAvatar2.png" width="52" height="52" style="max-width:52px" loading="lazy" alt="Community Answer"></picture>

									<div class="qa_user_name"></div>
				
									<div class="qa_user_label">Community Answer</div>
									
								</div>
							</div>
				
							<div class="qa_answer answer ">
								There are many scripts available on websites. Try searching for your favorite movie's script on-line. It may help to choose a movie you haven't yet seen and read the script first. After you watch the movie, you can compare the visuals of the actual movie to the script and get an understanding of the process of how the movie is made out of a script. 
							</div>

					<li id="qa_question_8" class="qa_aq qa_block " data-aqid="20908" data-cqid="20925" data-caid="21781" data-sqid="108911" data-qa_inactive="0" data-votes_up="148" data-votes_down="29" data-verifier_id="0" data-submitter_id="0">
					<div class="qa_divider"></div>
				
					<div class="qa_li_container">
						<div class="qa_question_tab">Question</div>
						<div class="qa_q_txt">Should I write an outline before writing a script?</div>
						
				
				
						<div class="qa_answers">
							<div class="qa_user_area">
								
				
								<div class="qa_user_hover hint_box">
										
										
								</div>
				
				
								<div class="qa_person_circle">
									<picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="/images/thumb/b/b0/CommunityAvatar2.png/-crop-104-104-104px-CommunityAvatar2.png.webp"><img src="/images/thumb/b/b0/CommunityAvatar2.png/-crop-104-104-104px-CommunityAvatar2.png" width="52" height="52" style="max-width:52px" loading="lazy" alt="Community Answer"></picture>
</div>
				
								<div class="qa_answerer_info">
				
									<div class="qa_user_name"></div>
				
									<div class="qa_user_label">Community Answer</div>
									
								</div>
							</div>
				
							<div class="qa_answer answer ">
								Yes, as it helps you to understand the entire story and the ending/consequences. Use paper and simply write the names of characters in a scene, then put the actions in bubbles around the paper and connect each character to a scene. From there, elaborate and add detail, as well as motives/POV for each character regarding the event.
							</div>
								<div class="qa_answer_footer">
									<div class="wh_vote_container qa_vote_buttons">
	<span class="wh_thumb_response wh_thumb_msg">Thanks!</span>
	<div class="qa_widget_vote_links">

		<a href="#" class="wh_vote_down wh_vote_box button secondary">No</a>
	</div>

		<a href="#" class="wh_vote_down wh_vote_box">Not Helpful <span>29</span></a>
		<a href="#" class="wh_vote_up wh_vote_box">Helpful <span>148</span></a>
	</div>
</div>



								</div>
						</div>
					</div>
				</li>
					<li id="qa_question_9" class="qa_aq qa_block " data-aqid="56929" data-cqid="56946" data-caid="57802" data-sqid="140953" data-qa_inactive="0" data-votes_up="131" data-votes_down="26" data-verifier_id="0" data-submitter_id="0">
					<div class="qa_divider"></div>
				
					<div class="qa_li_container">
						<div class="qa_question_tab">Question</div>
						<div class="qa_q_txt">What is the difference between writing a script and a story?</div>
						
				
				
						<div class="qa_answers">
							<div class="qa_user_area">
								
				
								<div class="qa_user_hover hint_box">
										
										
								</div>
				
				
								<div class="qa_person_circle">
									<picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="/images/thumb/f/f2/CommunityAvatar3.png/-crop-104-104-104px-CommunityAvatar3.png.webp"><img src="/images/thumb/f/f2/CommunityAvatar3.png/-crop-104-104-104px-CommunityAvatar3.png" width="52" height="52" style="max-width:52px" loading="lazy" alt="Community Answer"></picture>
</div>
				
								<div class="qa_answerer_info">
				
									<div class="qa_user_name"></div>
				
									<div class="qa_user_label">Community Answer</div>
									
								</div>
							</div>
				
							<div class="qa_answer answer ">
								A script is designed to be filmed. Therefore, the storytelling must be purely visual. If it can't be seen or heard, you don't write it down. A novel, on the other hand, is designed to be read. Therefore, the storytelling can be much more intimate, with plenty of time to express thoughts and feelings. 
							</div>
								<div class="qa_answer_footer">
									<div class="wh_vote_container qa_vote_buttons">
	<span class="wh_thumb_response wh_thumb_msg">Thanks!</span>
	<div class="qa_widget_vote_links">
		<a href="#" class="wh_vote_up wh_vote_box button secondary">Yes</a>
		<a href="#" class="wh_vote_down wh_vote_box button secondary">No</a>
	</div>
	<div class="qa_widget_vote_buttons">
		<a href="#" class="wh_vote_down wh_vote_box">Not Helpful <span>26</span></a>
		<a href="#" class="wh_vote_up wh_vote_box">Helpful <span>131</span></a>
	</div>
</div>



								</div>
						</div>
					</div>

<div class="section tips sticky">
<h2 class="section-heading block_header" onclick="javascript:mfTempOpenSection(2)">
<div class="altblock"></div>
<div class="mw-ui-icon mw-ui-icon-element indicator"></div>
<span class="mw-headline" id="Tips">Tips</span>
</h2>
<div id="tips" class="section_text">
<ul>
<li><div>There are no set rules to writing a screenplay. If you feel like your story should be told a different way, try them out.<div class="clearall"></div>
</div>
<div class="wh_vote_container">
	<span class="wh_thumb_response wh_thumb_msg">Thanks!</span>
	<div>
		<a href="#" class="trvote_up_2fbb7d226422d923bd8c6498ba4be558_1 vote_up wh_vote_box">
			Helpful
			<span class="tr_vote">0</span>
		</a>
		<a href="#" class="trvote_down_2fbb7d226422d923bd8c6498ba4be558_1 vote_down wh_vote_box">
			Not Helpful
			<span class="tr_vote">0</span>
		</a>
	</div>
</div>


</li>
<li><div>Read scripts to movies you enjoy to learn how they were written. Many PDFs can be found online with a simple search.<div class="clearall"></div>
</div>
<div class="wh_vote_container">
	<span class="wh_thumb_response wh_thumb_msg">Thanks!</span>
	<div>
		<a href="#" class="trvote_up_a47809a6147d3d4c93264baa08f69983_1 vote_up wh_vote_box">
			Helpful
			<span class="tr_vote">0</span>
		</a>
		<a href="#" class="trvote_down_a47809a6147d3d4c93264baa08f69983_1 vote_down wh_vote_box">
			Not Helpful
			<span class="tr_vote">0</span>
		</a>
	</div>
</div>


</li>
<li><div>Read books like <i>Save the Cat</i> by Blake Snyder or <i>Screenplay</i> by Syd Field to get ideas and information about how to format your stories.<div class="clearall"></div>
</div>
<div class="wh_vote_container">
	<span class="wh_thumb_response wh_thumb_msg">Thanks!</span>
	<div>
		<a href="#" class="trvote_up_d4a1a9d9c0dbfc0503e3a06279614782_1 vote_up wh_vote_box">
			Helpful
			<span class="tr_vote">0</span>
		</a>
		<a href="#" class="trvote_down_d4a1a9d9c0dbfc0503e3a06279614782_1 vote_down wh_vote_box">
			Not Helpful
			<span class="tr_vote">0</span>
		</a>
	</div>
</div>


</li>
<li><div>Stageplays and documentary scripts follow slightly different formats than a film or TV show script.<div class="clearall"></div>
</div>
<div class="wh_vote_container">
	<span class="wh_thumb_response wh_thumb_msg">Thanks!</span>
	<div>
		<a href="#" class="trvote_up_5065b0bebef66f0e7a2d81de31df5f83_1 vote_up wh_vote_box">
			Helpful
			<span class="tr_vote">0</span>
		</a>
		<a href="#" class="trvote_down_5065b0bebef66f0e7a2d81de31df5f83_1 vote_down wh_vote_box">
			Not Helpful
			<span class="tr_vote">0</span>
		</a>
	</div>
</div>


</li>
</ul>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</div>

<div id="summary_wrapper" class="section_text">
<a href="#summary_wrapper" class="collapse_link"><span id="summary_toc_heading_text">Article Summary</span><span id="summary_close">X</span></a><p class="text_summary_wrapper" id="summary_text">To write a script, always start with a scene heading that's aligned to the left margin whenever you go to a new location. You should also include action blocks whenever you want to describe the setting and character's actions, which should also be aligned with the left margin. For example, you might write, "John takes a sip of his coffee and smiles." When you want to include dialogue, center the character's name in all caps, and center the dialogue under their name. <span id="summary_last_sentence">To learn how to come up with a good story and realistic dialogue, read on!</span><span id="summary_position" class="sumpos_bottom"></span></p><div class="s-help-wrap" data-type="summarytexthelp">

Start taking inspiration from the world around you and ask yourself how it would be affected by a specific event or character. You may also think about an overall theme, such as love, family, or friendship for your story so that your whole script is tied together.\nFor example, \"What if you went back in time and met your parents when they were your age?\" is the premise for Back to the Future, while \"What if a monster rescued a princess instead of a handsome prince?\" is the premise to Shrek.\nCarry a small notebook with you wherever you go so you can take down notes when you get ideas.",

Look at the movies or TV shows that you enjoy most and try to write a script in a similar style.\nCombine genres to make something unique. For example, you may have a western movie that takes place in space or a romance movie with horror elements.\nPicking a Genre\nIf you like big set pieces and explosions, consider writing an action film.\nIf you want to scare other people, try writing a horror script.\nIf you want to tell a story about a relationship, try writing a drama or romantic comedy.\nIf you like a lot of special effects or what could happen in the future, write a science fiction film.",

                    "@type": "HowToStep",
                    "text": "Use high and low moments as your act breaks. Act breaks help separate your story into 3 parts: setup, confrontation, and resolution. The setup, or Act I, begins at the start of your story and ends when your character makes a choice that changes their lives forever. Throughout the confrontation, or Act II, your protagonist will work towards their goal and interact with your antagonist leading up to the climactic point of the story. The resolution, or Act III, takes place after the climax shows what happens afterward.Tip: TV scripts usually hit act breaks when they cut to commercials. Watch shows similar to the story you're writing to see what happens just before they go to a commercial break.",

Type the scene headings in all caps so they're easily recognizable. Include INT. or EXT. to tell readers if the scene takes place inside or outside.                     "@type": "HowToStep",
                    "text": "Write action blocks to describe settings and character actions. Action blocks should be aligned with the left margin and are written in regular sentence structure. Use action lines to denote what a character does and to give brief descriptions about what's happening. Keep action lines brief so they don't overwhelm a reader looking at the page.\nAvoid writing what the characters are thinking. A good rule of thumb to think about is if it can't be seen on a screen, don't include it in your action block. So instead of saying, \"John thinks about pulling the lever but he's not sure if he should,\" you may write something like, \"John's hand twitches near the lever. He grits his teeth and furrows his brow.\"\nWhen you introduce a character for the first time in an action block, use all caps for their name.             "acceptedAnswer": {
                "@type": "Answer",
                "text": "Usually with 2-3 lines of action or simple scene description work best when you're starting a new scene."
            }
        },
        {
            "@type": "Question",
            "name": "What the difference between documentary script format or commercial movies scripts?",
            "acceptedAnswer": {
                "@type": "Answer",
                "text": "Documentary scripts lay out what types of shots to get, such as nature footage or specific interviews. You can't plan for what an interviewee may say in a documentary, but you can plan out specific questions to help guide them toward the answers you want."
            }
        },
        {
            "@type": "Question",
            "name": "Is there any matter of light and camera in film script?",
            "acceptedAnswer": {
                "@type": "Answer",
                "text": "Usually, camera movements and lighting are used sparingly in a film script since that's the job of the director and director of photography on a film set."
            }
        }
    ]
